<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Emerging growth company&#160;<span id="xdx_90C_edei--EntityEmergingGrowthCompany_c20221110__20221110_zcm3uSM5wKMg"><ix:nonNumeric contextRef="From2022-11-10to2022-11-10" format="ixt:booleanfalse" name="dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany">&#9744;</ix:nonNumeric></span></p>

has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant
to Section 13(a) of the Exchange Act.&#160;&#9744;</p>

press release making the announcement is attached as Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form 8-K and is incorporated herein by reference.</p>

<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: right; background-color: white"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; background-color: white"><B>IT Tech Packaging,
Inc. Announces Third Quarter 2022 Unaudited Financial Results</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; background-color: white"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">BAODING,&nbsp;China,&nbsp;Nov.10,2022&nbsp;/PRNewswire/
--&nbsp;IT Tech Packaging, Inc. (NYSE American: ITP) (&ldquo;IT Tech Packaging&rdquo; or the &ldquo;Company&rdquo;), a leading manufacturer
and distributor of diversified paper products in&nbsp;North China, today announced its unaudited financial results for the three and nine
months ended September 30, 2022.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Mr. Zhenyong Liu, Chairman
and Chief Executive Officer of the Company, commented, &ldquo;Due to the sporadic situation of COVID-19 in China, the operation of our
factory facilities is highly restricted during the three months ended September 30, 2022. However, we still achieved a positive profit
year-on-year growth rate of 53% despite facing a volatile commodity price environment impacting our operating costs and the COVID-19 pandemic
lockout policies limiting our factory facilities operations. On the strategic front, we continued to deliver high-quality products to
our customers, strengthen our business operation, optimize the product portfolio, and seek significant economic benefits. Consistent with
our stated strategy, we continued to utilize excess cash flow in a balanced way to make investments in our long-term strategic growth
initiatives and to further strengthen the balance sheet. Looking forward, we are committed to creating value for its customers, employees,
shareholders, partners, industry, and society by seizing new opportunities and diversifying businesses.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>Third Quarter 2022
Unaudited Financial Results</B></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><I>Revenue</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">For the third quarter
of 2022, total revenue decreased by 29.7%, to&nbsp;approximately $31.71 million&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately $45.09 million&nbsp;for the
same period of last year. This was mainly due to the decrease in sales volume of regular CMP, offset printing paper and tissue paper products.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-right: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: left; background-color: white">The following table summarizes
revenue, volume and ASP by product for the third quarter of 2022 and 2021, respectively:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from CMP, including both regular CMP and
light-Weight CMP, decreased by 16.0%, to&nbsp;approximately $31.36 million&nbsp;and accounted for 98.9% of total revenue for the third
quarter of 2022, compared to&nbsp;approximately $37.33million, or 82.8% of total revenue for the same period of last year. The Company
sold 72,355 tonnes of CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$433/tonne in the third quarter of 2022, compared to 74,444&nbsp;tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$501/tonne
in the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Of the total CMP sales, revenue from regular CMP
decreased by 16.5%, to&nbsp;approximately $26.06 million for the third quarter of 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $31.20
million for the same period of last year. The Company sold 59,848 tonnesof regular CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$435/tonne during the third quarter
of 2022, compared to 61,947 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$504/tonne for the same period of last year. Revenue from light-weight CMP decreased
by 13.6%, to&nbsp;approximately $5.30 million for the third quarter of 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $6.13 million for
the same period of last year. The Company sold 12,507 tonnes of light-weight CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$423/tonne for the third quarter of
2022, compared to 12,497 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$490/tonne for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from offset printing paper was $nil&nbsp;for
the third quarter of 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately&nbsp;$4.80 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Revenue from tissue paper
products decreased by 89.6%, to&nbsp;approximately $0.29 million for the third quarter of 2022, from&nbsp;approximately&nbsp;$2.81 million&nbsp;for
the same period of last year. The Company sold 260tonnesof tissue paper products at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,128/tonne for the third quarter
of 2022, compared to 2,646 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,063/tonne for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Revenue from face masks
decreased by 62.6%, to&nbsp;approximately $0.06 million&nbsp;for the third quarter of 2022, from $0.15 million for the same period of
last year. The Company sold 1,282 thousand pieces of face masks for the third quarter of 2022, compared to3,180 thousand pieces of face
masks for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><I>Gross Profit and Gross
Margin</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Total cost of sales decreased by 33.1%, to&nbsp;approximately
$28.93 million&nbsp;for the third quarter of 2022 from&nbsp;approximately $43.27 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. This was
mainly due to the decrease in sales quantity of regular CMP, offset printing paper and tissue paper products, and the decrease in material
costs of CMP. Costs of sales per tonne for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, and &nbsp;&nbsp;tissue &nbsp;&nbsp;paper &nbsp;&nbsp;products were&nbsp;$388,&nbsp;$369,$nil
and&nbsp;$4,042, respectively, for the third quarter of 2022, compared to $489,&nbsp;$463,&nbsp;$570&nbsp;and&nbsp;$1,155, respectively,
for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Total gross profit was&nbsp;approximately $2.78
million&nbsp;for the third quarter of 2022, compared to the gross profit of&nbsp;approximately $1.82 million&nbsp;for the same period
of last year as a result of factors described above. Overall gross margin was 8.8% for the third quarter of 2022, compared to 4.0% for
the same period of last year. Gross profit(loss) margins for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, tissue paper products
and face mask products were 10.9%, 12.8%, nil%, -258.5% and 29.6%, respectively, for the third quarter of 2022, compared to 2.9%, 5.6%,
16.2%, -8.7% and 20.4%, respectively, for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>Selling, General and
Administrative Expenses</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Selling, general and
administrative expenses (&ldquo;SG&amp;A&rdquo;) increased by 66.9%, to&nbsp;approximately $3.37 million&nbsp;for the third quarter of 2022
from&nbsp;approximately $2.02million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>Loss from Operations</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Loss from operations
was&nbsp;approximately $0.59 million&nbsp;for the third quarter of 2022, a decrease of 197.3%, from loss from operations of&nbsp;approximately
$0.20 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. Operating loss margin was 1.9% for the third quarter of 2022, compared to operating
loss margin of 0.4% for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>Net Loss</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Net loss was&nbsp;approximately
$1.89 million, or loss per share of $0.03, for the third quarter of 2022, compared to net income of&nbsp;approximately $1.54 million,
or earnings per share of $0.03, for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>EBITDA</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">EBITDA was&nbsp;approximately
$2.43 million&nbsp;for the third quarter of 2022, compared to&nbsp;approximately $5.32 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Note 1: Non-GAAP Financial
Measures</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">In addition to our U.S.
GAAP results, this press release includes a discussion of EBITDA, a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by the Securities and Exchange
Commission (&ldquo;SEC&rdquo;). The Company defines EBITDA as net income before interest, income taxes, depreciation and amortization. EBITDA
is a key measure used by management to evaluate our results and make strategic decisions. Management believes this measure is useful to
investors because it is an indicator of operational performance. Because not all companies use identical calculations, the Company&rsquo;s presentation
of EBITDA may not be comparable to similarly titled measures of other companies, and should not be viewed as an alternative to measures
of financial performance or changes in cash flows calculated in accordance with the U.S. GAAP.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><I>Revenue</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">For the nine months ended
September 30, 2022, total revenue decreased by 31.8%, to&nbsp;approximately $78.98million&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately $115.83 million&nbsp;for
the same period of last year. This was mainly due to the decrease in sales volume of corrugating medium paper (&ldquo;CMP&rdquo;) and
offset printing paper and tissue paper products. The following table summarizes revenue, volume and ASP by product for the nine months
ended September 30, 2022 and 2021, respectively:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from CMP, including both regular CMP and
light-Weight CMP, decreased by 18.1%, to&nbsp;approximately $77.68 million&nbsp;and accounted for 98.3% of total revenue for nine months
ended September 30, 2022, compared to&nbsp;approximately $94.85 million, or 81.9% of total revenue for the same period of last year. The
Company sold 167,026tonnes of CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$465/tonne in nine months ended September 30, 2022, compared to 189,738&nbsp;tonnes
at an ASP of&nbsp;$500/tonne in the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Of the total CMP sales, revenue from regular CMP
decreased by 17.1%, to&nbsp;approximately $65.02 million for nine months ended September 30, 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately
$78.42million for the same period of last year. The Company sold 139,036tonnesof regular CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$468/tonne during the nine
months ended September 30, 2022, compared to 156,080 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$502/tonne for the same period of last year. Revenue from
light-weight CMP decreased by 23.0%, to&nbsp;approximately $12.66 million for the nine months ended September 30, 2022, compared to revenue
of&nbsp;approximately $16.44 million for the same period of last year. The Company sold 27,990 tonnes of light-weight CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$452/tonne
for the nine months ended September 30, 2022, compared to 33,658 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$488/tonne for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from offset printing paper was $nil&nbsp;for
the nine months ended September 30, 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately&nbsp;$14.10 million&nbsp;for the same period of last
year. The Company sold 20,602 tonnes of offset printing paper at an ASP of&nbsp;$684/tonne in the nine months ended September 30, 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Revenue from tissue paper
products decreased by 83.0%, to&nbsp;approximately $1.10million for the nine months ended September 30, 2022, from&nbsp;approximately&nbsp;$6.49
million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. The Company sold 1,040 tonnes of tissue paper products at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,061/tonne for
the nine months ended September 30, 2022, compared to 5,963 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,089/tonne for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Revenue from face masks
decreased by 48.7%, to&nbsp;approximately $0.20 million&nbsp;for the nine months ended September 30, 2022, from $0.39 million for the
same period of last year. The Company sold 4,295 thousand pieces of face masks for the nine months ended September 30, 2022, compared
to 9,650 thousand pieces of face masks for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><I>Gross Profit and Gross
Margin</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Total cost of sales decreased by 31.1%, to&nbsp;approximately
$75.25 million&nbsp;for the nine months ended September 30, 2022 from&nbsp;approximately $109.15 million&nbsp;for the same period of last
year. This was mainly a result of the decrease in sales volume of CMP and offset printing paper and decrease of material costs of CMP.
Costs of sales per tonne for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper and tissue paper products were&nbsp;$434,&nbsp;$411,$nil
and$3,114, respectively, for the nine months ended September 30, 2022, compared to $477,&nbsp;$453,&nbsp;$565 and&nbsp;$1,245, respectively,
for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Total gross profit was&nbsp;approximately $3.73million&nbsp;for
the nine months ended September 30, 2022, compared to the gross profit of&nbsp;approximately $6.68 million&nbsp;for the same period of
last year as a result of factors described above. Overall gross margin was 4.7% for the nine months ended September 30, 2022, compared
to 5.8% for the same period of last year. Gross profit(loss) margins for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, tissue
paper products and face mask products were 7.2%, 9.2%, nil%, -193.6%, and25.7%, respectively, for the nine months ended September 30,
2022, compared to 5.0%, 7.3%, 17.5%, -14.4% and 17.0%, respectively, for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>Selling, General and
Administrative Expenses</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Selling, general and
administrative expenses (&ldquo;SG&amp;A&rdquo;) increased by 19.1%, to&nbsp;approximately $8.54 million&nbsp;for the nine months ended
September 30, 2022 from&nbsp;approximately $7.17million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>Loss from Operations</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Loss from operations
was&nbsp;approximately $4.78 million&nbsp;for the nine months ended September 30, 2022, a decrease of 874.2%, from loss from operations
of&nbsp;approximately $0.49 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. Operating loss margin was 6.1% for the nine months ended September
30, 2022, compared to operating loss margin of 0.4% for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><I>Net Loss</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Net loss was&nbsp;approximately
$4.66 million, or loss per share of $0.07, for the nine months ended September 30, 2022, compared to net loss of&nbsp;approximately $3.25
million, or loss per share of $0.06, for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>EBITDA</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">EBITDA was&nbsp;approximately
$7.18 million&nbsp;for the nine months ended September 30, 2022, compared to&nbsp;approximately $2.69 million&nbsp;for the same period
of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Note 1: Non-GAAP Financial
Measures</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">In addition to our U.S.
GAAP results, this press release includes a discussion of EBITDA, a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by the Securities and Exchange
Commission (&ldquo;SEC&rdquo;). The Company defines EBITDA as net income before interest, income taxes, depreciation and amortization. EBITDA
is a key measure used by management to evaluate our results and make strategic decisions. Management believes this measure is useful to
investors because it is an indicator of operational performance. Because not all companies use identical calculations, the Company&rsquo;s presentation
of EBITDA may not be comparable to similarly titled measures of other companies, and should not be viewed as an alternative to measures
of financial performance or changes in cash flows calculated in accordance with the U.S. GAAP.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>Cash, Liquidity and
Financial Position</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">As of&nbsp;September 30, 2022, the Company had
cash and bank balances, short-term debt (including bank loans, current portion of long-term loans from credit union and related party
loans), and long-term debt (including related party loans) of&nbsp;approximately $16.02million,&nbsp;$10.54 million and&nbsp;$4.69 million,
respectively, compared to approximately$11.20&nbsp;million,&nbsp;$13.52&nbsp;million and&nbsp;$2.98 million, respectively, as of&nbsp;December
31, 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Net accounts receivable
was&nbsp;approximately $4.24&nbsp;million as of September 30, 2022, compared to approximately&nbsp;$4.87&nbsp;million as of&nbsp;December
31, 2021. Net inventory was approximately&nbsp;$4.44&nbsp;million as of&nbsp;September 30, 2022, compared to&nbsp;approximately$5.84&nbsp;million
as of&nbsp;December 31, 2021. As of&nbsp;September 30, 2022, the Company had current assets of&nbsp;approximately$48.43&nbsp;million and
current liabilities of&nbsp;approximately$17.59million, resulting in a working capital of&nbsp;approximately$30.84&nbsp;million. This
was compared to current assets of approximately $55.52 million and current liabilities of approximately $20.43 million, resulting in a
working capital of approximately $35.09 million as of&nbsp;December 31, 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Net cash provided by operating activities was&nbsp;approximately$7.43
million&nbsp;for the nine months ended September 30, 2022, compared to net cash used in operating activities of approximately&nbsp;$6.44
million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. Net cash used in investing activities was&nbsp;approximately$8.19 million&nbsp;for the
nine months ended September 30, 2022, compared to approximately$12.78 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. Net cash provided
by financing activities was&nbsp;approximately$6.84million&nbsp;for the nine months ended September 30, 2022, compared to approximately$41.55
million for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>About IT Tech Packaging,
Inc.</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Founded in 1996, IT Tech
Packaging, Inc. is a leading manufacturer and distributor of diversified paper products in North China. Using recycled paper as its primary
raw material (with the exception of its tissue paper products), ITP produces and distributes three categories of paper products: corrugating
medium paper, offset printing paper and tissue paper products. With production based in Baoding and Xingtai in North China&rsquo;s Hebei Province,
ITP is located strategically close to the Beijing and Tianjin region, home to a growing base of industrial and manufacturing activities
and one of the largest markets for paper products consumption in the country. ITP has been listed on the NYSE American since December
2009. For more information, please visit:&nbsp;http://www.itpackaging.cn/.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>
